holoclar is a two - step procedure . it is used to remove the outer layer of the eye . holloclar consists of two steps : 1 - biopsy . this is referred to as a biopsy , which is based on the presence of limbal cells in the eye and a biopsy to check for the presence and function of these cells . the biopsy is performed using eye - drops to anaesthetise in the outer layers of the cornea . after the biopsies , the biophysies are performed , this biopsy will be performed with antibiotics to treat an infection . 2 - holaclar implantation is performed with anaesthesia and eye removal from the cornea on day of surgery . day of operation , anaesthetic is used for eye removal .
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . most side effects affect the eye after the surgery . the effects usually disappear in the first few days after surgery , but may be temporary . if you experience any of the following side effects after surgery or after surgery you may experience some of the side effects listed below : cornea ( erosion ) or perforation of the cornea . this may occur within 3 months after holoclar implantation . these may affect up to 1 in 10 people . inflammation of the eyelids ( blepharitis ) may affect more than 1 in 100 people , if bleeding occurs during the operation . bleeding may occur in patients who have had surgery if they have had any of these side effects during the surgery or have had a history of bleeding during the procedure . you should tell your doctor immediately if any of them happen .
